Examples of categories are 3 of a kind, 4 of a kind,\r\nstraight, full house, etc. Each player tries to fill in a score for each category, but this is\r\nnot always possible. When players have entered a score or a zero for all 13 categories,\r\nthe game ends and total scores are compared.\r\n\r\nSpecial Yatzy rule is, the first time you get a yatzy in a game it is worth 50 points (if\r\nyou use it in the yatzy slot).
